# <a name="essential-services-for-office"></a><span data-ttu-id="9847d-103">Ključni servisi za Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-103">Essential services for Office</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="9847d-104">Informacije u ovom članku odnose se na verziju 1904 ili noviju verziju sljedećeg klijentskog softvera sustava Office instaliranog na računalu sa sustavom Windows:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-104">The information in this article applies to Version 1904 or later of the following Office client software installed on a computer running Windows:</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-105">Office 365 ProPlus i Office 365 Business</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-105">Office 365 ProPlus and Office 365 Business</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-106">Office 365 Personal, Office 365 Home ili druge verzije sustava Office koje su dio pretplate na Office 365.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-106">Office 365 Personal, Office 365 Home, or other versions of Office that are part of an Office 365 subscription.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-107">Project i Visio koji se isporučuju s nekim pretplatničkim tarifama, kao što su Project Online Professional ili Visio Online Plan 2.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-107">Project and Visio that come with some subscription plans, such as the Project Online Professional plan or Visio Online Plan 2.</span></span>


<span data-ttu-id="9847d-108">Office se sastoji od klijentskih softverskih aplikacija i povezanih okruženja osmišljenih radi učinkovitijeg stvaranja, komunikacije i suradnje.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-108">Office consists of client software applications and connected experiences designed to enable you to create, communicate, and collaborate more effectively.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9847d-109">Premda kao administrator tvrtke ili ustanove možete upravljati brojnim povezanim sučeljima koja su dostupna vama ili vašim korisnicima, neki su servisi ključni za funkcioniranje sustava Office, pa se ne mogu onemogućiti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-109">While you can control many of the connected experiences that are available to you, or to your users if you’re the admin in your organization, there are a set of services that are essential to how Office functions and therefore cannot be disabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9847d-110">To je, primjerice, servis za licenciranje, koji potvrđuje da imate odgovarajuću licencu za korištenje sustava Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-110">For example, the licensing service that confirms that you are properly licensed to use Office.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9847d-111">Obavezni servisni podaci o tim servisima prikupljaju se i šalju Microsoftu bez obzira na druge konfigurirane postavke zaštite privatnosti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-111">Required service data about these services is collected and sent to Microsoft, regardless of any other privacy-related policy settings that you have configured.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9847d-112">Te podatke možete pogledati pomoću preglednika dijagnostičkih podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-112">You can see this data by using the Diagnostic Data Viewer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-113">Dodatne informacije potražite u sljedećim člancima:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-113">For more information, see the following:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="9847d-114">Obavezni servisni podaci za Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-114">Required service data for Office</span></span>](required-service-data.md)
- [<span data-ttu-id="9847d-115">Korištenje preglednika dijagnostičkih podataka sa sustavom Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-115">Using the Diagnostic Data Viewer with Office</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/cf761ce9-d805-4c60-a339-4e07f3182855)
- [<span data-ttu-id="9847d-116">Povezana okruženja u sustavu Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-116">Connected experiences in Office</span></span>](connected-experiences.md)

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-117">Ako ste administrator za tvrtku ili ustanovu, možda će vas zanimati i sljedeći članci:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-117">If you’re the admin for your organization, you might also be interested in the following:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="9847d-118">Pregled kontrola za zaštitu privatnosti za Office 365 ProPlus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-118">Overview of privacy controls for Office 365 ProPlus</span></span>](overview-privacy-controls.md)
- [<span data-ttu-id="9847d-119">Korištenje postavki pravilnika za upravljanje kontrolama za zaštitu privatnosti za Office 365 ProPlus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-119">Use policy settings to manage privacy controls for Office 365 ProPlus</span></span>](manage-privacy-controls.md)

## <a name="list-of-essential-services-for-office"></a><span data-ttu-id="9847d-120">Popis ključnih servisa za Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-120">List of essential services for Office</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-121">U tablici u nastavku naveden je popis ključnih servisa za Office i opis svakog servisa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-121">The following table provides a list of the essential services for Office and a description of each service.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="9847d-122">**Servis**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-122">**Service**</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="9847d-123">**Opis**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-123">**Description**</span></span>  |
| ------ | ---- |
| [<span data-ttu-id="9847d-124">Provjera autentičnosti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-124">Authentication</span></span>](#authentication-events) | <span data-ttu-id="9847d-125">Provjera autentičnosti servis je koji obuhvaća više platformi, a služi za provjeru valjanosti identiteta korisnika sustava Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-125">Authentication is a cross-platform service that validates your Office user identity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9847d-126"> Nužan je da biste se mogli prijaviti u Office, aktivirati licencu za Office, pristupiti datotekama pohranjenima u oblaku, a omogućuje i dosljedno sučelje u svim sesijama sustava Office na svim uređajima.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-126"> It is required to enable you to sign in to Office, activate your Office license, access your files stored in the cloud, and provides a consistent experience across Office sessions and your devices.</span></span>    |
| [<span data-ttu-id="9847d-127">Klikom do cilja</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-127">Click-to-Run</span></span>](#click-to-run-events) | <span data-ttu-id="9847d-128">"Klikom do cilja" tehnologija je za instalaciju koja se koristi za instaliranje i ažuriranje sustava Office u sustavu Windows.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-128">Click-to-Run is the installation technology used to install and update Office on Windows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9847d-129">Tehnologija provjerava postoji li nova verzija sustava Office i kad postoji, preuzima je i instalira.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-129">It checks for new versions of Office, and when a new version is available, downloads and installs it.</span></span><span data-ttu-id="9847d-130"> Tehnologija "klikom do cilja" otkrit će jesu li vam potrebna ažuriranja sustava Office, uključujući sigurnosna ažuriranja, te će ih preuzeti i instalirati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-130"> Click-to-Run will detect the need for, perform the download of, and install Office updates, including security updates.</span></span>     |
| [<span data-ttu-id="9847d-131">Servis za poboljšanu konfiguraciju (eng. Enhanced Configuration Service, ECS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-131">Enhanced Configuration Service (ECS)</span></span>](#experimentation-and-configuration-service-ecs-events) | <span data-ttu-id="9847d-132">ECS Microsoftu omogućuje da iznova konfigurira instalacije sustava Office bez potrebe za ponovnom implementacijom sustava.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-132">ECS provides Microsoft the ability to reconfigure Office installations without the need for you to redeploy Office.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9847d-133">Služi za kontroliranje postupnog objavljivanja značajki ili ažuriranja, a učinak objavljivanja prati se na temelju prikupljenih dijagnostičkih podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-133">It is used to control the gradual rollout of features or updates, while the impact of the rollout is monitored from diagnostic data being collected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9847d-134">Koristi se i za ublažavanje sigurnosnih problema i problema s performansama neke značajke ili ažuriranja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-134">It is also used to mitigate security or performance issues with a feature or update.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9847d-135">ECS podržava i promjene konfiguracije povezane s dijagnostičkim podacima da bi se prikupljali odgovarajući događaji.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-135">In addition, ECS supports configuration changes related to diagnostic data to help ensure that the appropriate events are being collected.</span></span> |
| [<span data-ttu-id="9847d-136">Licenciranje</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-136">Licensing</span></span>](#licensing-events)     | <span data-ttu-id="9847d-137">Licenciranje je servis u oblaku koji podržava aktivaciju novih instalacija sustava Office te održava licencu na uređajima nakon aktivacije sustava.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-137">Licensing is a cloud-based service that supports your Office activation for new installations and maintains the license on your devices after Office has been activated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9847d-138">Servis registrira svaki uređaj i aktivira Office, provjerava status pretplate na Office te upravlja ključevima proizvoda.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-138">It registers each of your devices and activates Office, checks the status of your Office subscription, and manages your product keys.</span></span>    |
| [<span data-ttu-id="9847d-139">Konfiguracija servisa</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-139">Services Configuration</span></span>](#services-configuration-events)  | <span data-ttu-id="9847d-140">Konfiguracija servisa omogućuje ažuriranje postavki konfiguracije sustava Office radi omogućivanja odnosno onemogućivanja značajki klijenata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-140">Services Configuration provides the ability to make updates to Office configuration settings to enable or disable client features.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9847d-141">Aktivira se svaki put kad se pokrene neka aplikacija sustava Office te sadrži pojedinosti o drugim konfiguracijama i servisima sustava Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-141">It is called every time an Office application is started and provides details about other Office configurations and services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9847d-142">Konfiguracija servisa ujedno kontrolira koji su servisi određeni kao ključni.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-142">Services Configuration also controls which services are designated as essential services.</span></span>  |
| [<span data-ttu-id="9847d-143">Telemetrija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-143">Telemetry </span></span>](#telemetry-events)  | <span data-ttu-id="9847d-144">Servis za telemetriju služi za prikupljanje dijagnostičkih podataka iz aplikacija sustava Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-144">The Telemetry service is used to collect diagnostic data from Office applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9847d-145">Omogućuje prikupljanje obaveznih i neobaveznih dijagnostičkih podataka koje je generirao Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-145">It enables the collection of the diagnostic data generated by Office, both required and optional diagnostic data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9847d-146">Odgovoran je i za prikupljanje onog dijela obaveznih servisnih podataka za Office koji obuhvaća servisne dijagnostičke podatke.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-146">It is also responsible for the collection of the service diagnostic data portion of required service data for Office.</span></span>  |

## <a name="events-and-data-fields-for-essential-services-for-office"></a><span data-ttu-id="9847d-147">Događaji i podatkovna polja za ključne servise za Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-147">Events and data fields for essential services for Office</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-148">U sljedećim odjeljcima navode se ove informacije:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-148">The next sections provide the following information:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9847d-149">popis događaja za svaki ključni servis</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-149">A list of events for each essential service</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="9847d-150">opis svakog događaja</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-150">A description of each event</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="9847d-151">popis podatkovnih polja u svakom događaju</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-151">A list of data fields in each event</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="9847d-152">opis svakog podatkovnog polja</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-152">A description of each data field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-153">Događaje možete pogledati pomoću preglednika dijagnostičkih podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-153">You can see these events by using the Diagnostic Data Viewer.</span></span>



## <a name="authentication-events"></a><span data-ttu-id="9847d-154">Događaji provjere autentičnosti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-154">Authentication events</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-155">Ti se događaji dijagnostičkih podataka prikupljaju kada Office pokuša dohvatiti token za provjeru autentičnosti, bilo u pozadini ili putem upita korisniku.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-155">These diagnostic data events are collected when Office attempts to acquire an authentication token, either silently or through prompting.</span></span>

### <a name="officeidentityfbapromptwin32"></a><span data-ttu-id="9847d-156">Office.Identity.FbaPromptWin32</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-156">Office.Identity.FbaPromptWin32</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-157">Prikuplja se kada Office korisniku prikaže upit za prijavu pomoću provjere autentičnosti na temelju obrazaca.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-157">Collected when Office shows the user a Forms-Based-Auth sign-in prompt.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-158">Upiti za provjeru autentičnosti zajedno s pozadinskim pribavljanjem tokena koriste se za utvrđivanje je li korisnik u neispravnom stanju provjere autentičnosti, koje se za korisnika očituje praktički izvanmrežnim stanjem klijenta. Neispravna provjera autentičnosti može i onemogućiti dohvaćanje licence, što uzrokuje potpunu nemogućnost korištenja klijenta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-158">Along with silent token acquisitions, authentication prompts is used to determine if user is in a broken authentication state which, for the user, results in what is essentially an Offline Client state, or in the worst case, broken authentication may prevent license acquisition and result in a completely unusable client.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-159">Upiti za prijavu pomoću provjere autentičnosti na temelju obrazaca (FBA) koriste se u nekim scenarijima lokalne provjere autentičnosti i najčešće ne želimo da se to događa jer bi svi trebali koristiti modernu provjeru autentičnosti zbog sigurnosnih slabih točaka povezanih s provjerom autentičnosti na temelju obrazaca.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-159">Forms-Based-Auth (FBA) sign-in prompts are used for some on-premises authentication scenarios and typically we want to make sure this isn’t happening, as everyone should be using Modern-Auth because of security vulnerabilities associated with FBA.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-160">**Prikupljaju se sljedeća polja:**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-160">**The following fields are collected:**</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-161">**AuthScheme** – korištena shema provjere autentičnosti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-161">**AuthScheme** - the authentication scheme used</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-162">**DocumentUrlHash** – šifrirano slanje zahtjeva za URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-162">**DocumentUrlHash** - an encrypted URL requesting</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-163">**EndTag** – oznaka ispunjenosti FPA obrasca</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-163">**EndTag** - the tag where FBA form is completed</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-164">**Flags** – zastarjelo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-164">**Flags** - Obsolete</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-165">**FlowTag** – oznaka pokretanja FBA obrasca</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-165">**FlowTag** - the tag where FBA form is started</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-166">**LastError** – vraćena šifra pogreške</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-166">**LastError** – the error code returned</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-167">**PromptEndTime** – vrijeme završetka upita</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-167">**PromptEndTime** - the time when then prompt ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-168">**PromptStartTime** – vrijeme početka upita</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-168">**PromptStartTime** - the time when the prompt started</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-169">**Result** – označava je li provjera autentičnosti uspjela</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-169">**Result** - whether the authentication succeeded</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-170">**SessionEndTime** – vrijeme završetka sesije događaja</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-170">**SessionEndTime** – the time when the event session ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-171">**Timeout** – vrijeme isteka vremena upita</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-171">**Timeout** - the time when the prompt timed out</span></span>

### <a name="officeidentitysignoutevent"></a><span data-ttu-id="9847d-172">Office.Identity.SignOutEvent</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-172">Office.Identity.SignOutEvent</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-173">Prikuplja se kad se korisnik odjavi iz sustava Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-173">Collected when a user signs out of Office.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-174">Kad se zna da se korisnik odjavio, moguće je na očekivani način klasificirati druge događaje, kao što su upiti, da bi se točno izračunali u metrici pouzdanosti / spremnosti za isporuku te se izbjegavaju upozorenja ili vraćanje međuverzija na temelju pogrešne premise da se korisniku prikazuju neočekivani upiti za prijavu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-174">Knowing the user is signed-out makes it possible to classify other events, such as prompts, as expected, so those events can be correctly computed in reliability / ship-readiness metrics and avoid alerting or rolling back builds on the faulty premise that the user is experiencing unexpected sign-in prompts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-175">Prikupljaju se sljedeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-175">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-176">**FlowEndTime** – vrijeme završetka radnje odjave</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-176">**FlowEndTime** - the time when the sign out action ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-177">**FlowStartTime** – vrijeme početka radnje odjave</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-177">**FlowStartTime** - the time when the sign out action started</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-178">**IdentityErrorState** – bilo koje stanje pogreške identiteta tijekom odjave</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-178">**IdentityErrorState** - any identity error state during sign out</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-179">**IdentityHashedUniqueId** – šifrirani ID identiteta koji se odjavljuje</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-179">**IdentityHashedUniqueId** - the encrypted identity ID being signed out</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-180">**IdentityProviderType** – davatelj identiteta koji se odjavljuje</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-180">**IdentityProviderType** - the identity provider of the identity being signed out</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-181">**IdentityUniqueID** – ID identiteta koji se odjavljuje</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-181">**IdentityUniqueID** - the identity ID being signed out</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-182">**SessionEndTime** – vrijeme završetka sesije događaja</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-182">**SessionEndTime** - the time when the event session ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-183">**SignOutUserAction** – označava da je korisnik pokrenuo radnju odjave</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-183">**SignOutUserAction** - Indicates the user initiates the sign out action</span></span>

### <a name="officeidentitysspipromptwin32"></a><span data-ttu-id="9847d-184">Office.Identity.SspiPromptWin32</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-184">Office.Identity.SspiPromptWin32</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-185">Prikuplja se kada Office korisniku prikaže upit za prijavu putem Windows SSPI-ja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-185">Collected when Office shows the user a Windows SSPI sign-in prompt.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9847d-186">Upiti za provjeru autentičnosti zajedno s pozadinskim pribavljanjem tokena određuju je li korisnik u neispravnom stanju provjere autentičnosti, koje se očituje izvanmrežnim stanjem klijenta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-186">Along with silent token acquisitions, authentication prompts determine whether a user is in a broken authentication state, which results in an Offline Client state.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9847d-187">Neispravna provjera autentičnosti može i onemogućiti dohvaćanje licence, što uzrokuje potpunu nemogućnost korištenja klijenta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-187">Broken authentication may prevent license acquisition and result in a completely unusable client.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-188">Upiti Windows SSPI-ja koriste se za provjeru autentičnosti u sustavu Exchange (za sinkronizaciju pošte) kad korisnikov resurs sustava Exchange nije postavljen za višestruku provjeru autentičnosti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-188">Windows SSPI prompts are used for authenticating with Exchange (for mail synchronizing) when the user's Exchange resource hasn't been setup for multi-factor authentication.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-189">Ti događaji, zajedno s događajima prostora za naziv Office.MATS, koriste se u sljedeće svrhe:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-189">These events, along with the Office.MATS namespace events, are used for the following purposes:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-190">1\) utvrđivanje mogu li klijenti uspješno dohvatiti token za provjeru autentičnosti ili su prešli u stanje neispravne provjere autentičnosti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-190">1\) Identify whether clients can successfully obtain an authentication token or have entered a broken authentication state.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-191">2\) procjenu jesu li promjene u klijentu ili servisu uzrokovale kritično nazadovanje sučelja i pouzdanosti provjere autentičnosti korisnika</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-191">2\) Evaluate whether changes that have occurred on the client or services have resulted in critical regressions in the user's authentication experience and reliability</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-192">3\) u slučaju pogrešaka ti signali šalju važne šifre pogrešaka iz odgovorne komponente (koda klijentskog programa sustava Office, biblioteka za provjeru autentičnosti ili servisa izdavatelja certifikata) koje se mogu koristiti za klasifikaciju hitnosti, dijagnozu i otklanjanje problema</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-192">3\) When failures occur, these signals emit important failure codes from the responsible component (Office client code, authentication libraries, or authority services) which can be used for triage, diagnosis and mitigation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-193">4\) signali služe kao podaci za razne nadzornike spremnosti za isporuku i stanja koji aktiviraju upozorenja da bi se naši inženjeri mogli brzo angažirati i skratiti vrijeme do otklanjanje kritičnih pogrešaka koje blokiraju rad korisnika</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-193">4\) These signals power various ship readiness and health monitors which fire alerts so our engineers can engage quickly and reduce the time to mitigation of critical user-blocking failures</span></span>

### <a name="officematsactionofficewin32-officematsactionofficewinrt"></a><span data-ttu-id="9847d-244">Office.MATS.actionofficewin32, Office.MATS.actionofficewinrt</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-244">Office.MATS.actionofficewin32, Office.MATS.actionofficewinrt</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-245">Sljedeći se opis odnosi i na Win32 događaje i na WinRT događaje (naziv ovisi o platformi)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-245">The following description applies for both Win32 and WinRT events (the name depends on platform.)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-246">Microsoft Auth Telemetry System (MATS) prikuplja se kada Office pokuša dohvatiti token za provjeru autentičnosti, bilo u pozadini ili putem upita korisniku.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-246">Microsoft Auth Telemetry System (MATS) is collected when Office attempts to acquire an authentication token, either silently or through prompting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9847d-247">Kada pokušaj dohvaćanja ne uspije, uvrštavaju se informacije o pogrešci.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-247">When acquisition attempts fail, error information is included.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9847d-248">Korisnici pomoću tih događaja mogu izbjeći prelazak u stanje neispravne provjere autentičnosti tako što:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-248">These events help our users avoid entering broken authentication states by:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-249">1\) utvrde mogu li klijenti uspješno dohvatiti token za provjeru autentičnosti ili su prešli u stanje neispravne provjere autentičnosti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-249">1\) Identifying whether clients can successfully obtain an authentication token or have entered a broken authentication state.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-250">2\) procijene uzrokuju li promjene u klijentu ili servisu kritično nazadovanje sučelja i pouzdanosti provjere autentičnosti korisnika</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-250">2\) Evaluate when changes occur on the client or services, whether they result in critical regressions in the user's authentication experience and reliability</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-251">3\) u slučaju pogrešaka ti signali šalju važne šifre pogrešaka iz odgovorne komponente (koda klijentskog programa sustava Office, biblioteka za provjeru autentičnosti ili servisa izdavatelja certifikata) koje se mogu koristiti za klasifikaciju hitnosti, dijagnozu i otklanjanje problema</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-251">3\) When failures occur, these signals emit important failure codes from the responsible component (Office client code, authentication libraries, or authority services) which can be used for triage, diagnosis and mitigation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-252">4\) signali služe kao podaci za razne nadzornike spremnosti za isporuku i stanja koji aktiviraju upozorenja da bi se naši inženjeri mogli brzo angažirati i skratiti vrijeme do otklanjanje kritičnih pogrešaka</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-252">4\) These signals power various ship readiness and health monitors which fire alerts so our engineers can engage quickly and reduce the time to mitigation of critical failures.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9847d-253">Prikupljaju se sljedeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-253">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-254">**Actiontype** – označava koja se biblioteka provjere autentičnosti koristi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-254">**Actiontype** - Which authentication library is used</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-255">**Appaudience** – označava je li međuverzija aplikacije za internu ili vanjsku upotrebu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-255">**Appaudience** - Is the app build for internal or external use</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-256">**Appforcedprompt** – označava je li aplikacija nadjačala predmemoriju i prisilno prikazala upit</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-256">**Appforcedprompt** - Did the app override cache and force a prompt to be shown</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-257">**Appname** – naziv aplikacije koja provodi provjeru autentičnosti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-257">**Appname** - Name of the application doing authentication</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-258">**Appver** – verzija aplikacije koja provodi provjeru autentičnosti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-258">**Appver** - Version of the application doing authentication</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-259">**Askedforcreds** – označava je li aplikacija od korisnika tražila unos vjerodajnica za tu radnju</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-259">**Askedforcreds** - Did the application ask the user to enter credentials for this action</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-260">**Authoutcome** – označava uspjeh, neuspjeh ili otkazivanje provjere autentičnosti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-260">**Authoutcome** - Did the authentication attempt succeed, fail, or was cancelled</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-261">**Blockingprompt** – označava je li aplikacija izbacila upit na koji korisnik mora reagirati</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-261">**Blockingprompt** - Did the application throw a prompt requiring user interaction</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-262">**Correlationid** – GUID korišten za spajanje sa servisnim podacima</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-262">**Correlationid** - GUID used for joining with services data</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-338">**Scenarioid** – GUID.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-338">**Scenarioid** – GUID.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9847d-339">U jednom scenariju može biti veći broj događaja, npr. scenarijem se može dodavati novi račun, ali se u sklopu njega prikazuje više upita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-339">Multiple events may belong to a single scenario, e.g. the scenario may be adding a new account but there are multiple prompts that occur as part of that scenario.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9847d-340">Taj ID omogućuje korelaciju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-340">This ID enables correlation to happen.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-342">**Skdver** –verzija SDK-a MATS klijenta koja je korištena za stvaranje podataka</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-342">**Skdver** - Version of MATS client SDK used to produce this data</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-343">**StartTime** – vrijeme pozivanja MATS API-ja Start\*Action</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-343">**Starttime** - Time at which the Start\*Action MATS API was called</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-344">**Tenantid** – GUID koji označava klijent kojem korisnik provjerene autentičnosti pripada (u slučajevima koji nisu ADAL).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-344">**Tenantid** - GUID identifying the tenant the authenticated user belongs to (in non-ADAL cases).</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-345">**Uploadid** – jedinstveni GUID događaja, koristi se za poništavanje dupliciranja</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-345">**Uploadid** - Unique GUID for this event, used for de-duping</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-346">**Wamapi** – određuje koji se WAM API poziva</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-346">**Wamapi** - Identifies which WAM API is called</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9847d-347">**Wamtelemetrybatch** – trenutno se ne koristi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-347">**Wamtelemetrybatch** - Currently unused.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9847d-348">Ubuduće će komponenti WAM omogućiti slanje dodatnih informacija o događaju provjere autentičnosti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9847d-348">In the future, allows the WAM component to dispatch additional information regarding the authentication event.</span></span>
